country_event = {
	id = 300017
	title = "Dynamic Loc Province Selection Renaming"
	desc = ""
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_province value = 0.9 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_province value = 1.1 } }
				}
			}
			dynamic_loc_slot_1 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = dynamic_loc_slot_selector
					duration = 1
				}
			}
			random_neighbor_province = {
				limit = { has_province_modifier = dynamic_loc_potential_province_target }
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = dynamic_loc_province_target_1
					duration = -1
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = dynamic_loc_slot_selector
					duration = -1
				}
				remove_province_modifier = dynamic_loc_potential_province_target
			}
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_province value = 1.9 }
					NOT = { check_variable = { which = dynamic_loc_names_province value = 2.1 } }
				}
			}
			dynamic_loc_slot_2 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = dynamic_loc_slot_selector
					duration = 1
				}
			}
